module testbench;
reg  clk;
reg  areset;
reg  bump_left;
reg  bump_right;
reg  ground;
reg  dig;
wire  walk_left;
wire  walk_right;
wire  aaah;
wire  digging;

integer file, scenario;
// DUT instantiation
top_module DUT (
	.clk(clk),
	.areset(areset),
	.bump_left(bump_left),
	.bump_right(bump_right),
	.ground(ground),
	.dig(dig),
	.walk_left(walk_left),
	.walk_right(walk_right),
	.aaah(aaah),
	.digging(digging)
);
// Clock generation
initial begin
    clk = 0;
    forever #5 clk = ~clk;
end

initial begin
    file = $fopen("TBout.txt", "w");
end
// Scenario Based Test
initial begin

    // scenario 1: Asynchronous reset: assert areset = 1 at t=0, hold ≥2 cycles; deassert at rising edge of clk at t=3

reg  bump_right;

	.clk(clk),
	.areset(areset),
	.bump_left(bump_left),
	.bump_right(bump_right),

	.dig(dig),

);

// DUT instantiation

	.clk(clk),
	.areset(areset),
	.bump_left(bump_left),
	.bump_right(bump_right),
	.ground(ground),
	.dig(dig),

);

reg  clk;
reg  areset;
reg  bump_left;
reg  bump_right;
reg  ground;

wire  walk_right;

// DUT instantiation

	.clk(clk),
	.areset(areset),
	.bump_left(bump_left),
	.bump_right(bump_right),
	.ground(ground),
	.dig(dig),

);

end

    file = $fopen("TBout.txt", "w");
end
// Scenario Based Test
initial begin

    areset = 1; bump_left = 0; bump_right = 0; ground = 0; dig = 0;
    #10;

reg  clk;
reg  areset;
reg  bump_left;
reg  bump_right;
reg  ground;

wire  walk_left;
wire  walk_right;

wire  digging;

integer file, scenario;
// DUT instantiation
top_module DUT (
	.clk(clk),
	.areset(areset),
	.bump_left(bump_left),
	.bump_right(bump_right),
	.ground(ground),
	.dig(dig),
	.walk_left(walk_left),
	.walk_right(walk_right),
	.aaah(aaah),
	.digging(digging)
);
// Clock generation

    clk = 0;
    forever #5 clk = ~clk;
end

    file = $fopen("TBout.txt", "w");
end
